The benefits and convenience of mineral sprays are undisputed - you can all agree on that right? Mineral sprays come in various sizes, small ones are easy to bring to school, work, travel, and the main purpose is to moisturize/provide extra hydration to the skin anytime, anywhere. Famous and popular mineral sprays like Avene or Evian are spring water/mineral water types. I'm not saying these brands are not good because I'm currently using Avene and like it a lot.\n\nThe difference that made me choose to buy Caudalie Grape Water first (the first mist I've ever had) is that its spray contains 100% extract from organic grapes. Reading the promotional section, I must say it sounds very \"bombastic\" but looking at the back label, I see it says \"USDA Certified Biobased Product - 97%\"... so does this mean the product is only 97% pure extract from grapes? I feel I like this Caudalie Grape Water spray more than other types because the grape extract makes me immediately think of the antioxidant effect for skin that grapes provide. Just from spraying I feel at least this type of water has some added superior effects over others (even if it doesn't contain 100% grape extract >.<) When spraying it feels like a fine mist, it's hard to detect the grape scent but in comparison with Avene, I can feel Caudalie Grape Water is slightly more refreshing (or maybe I'm too swayed by the \"100% extract from grapes\" claim ^^ ) The water droplets spray a little \"stronger\" than the Avene bottle but still super gentle on skin. Absorption is quite fast (almost instant) leaving skin feeling much more \"moist\". Some ways to use this mineral spray (you can definitely apply these to other mineral sprays too):\n\n + You can spray after cleansing and before applying moisturizer.
